d":"10","name":"\u015amieszne","ec2":"smieszne"},{"id":"11","name":"Miasta-Pa\u0144stwa","ec2":"miasta_panstwa"},{"id":"12","name":"Ro\u015blinki","ec2":"roslinki"},{"id":"3","name":"\u015awi\u0105teczne","ec2":"swiateczne"},{"id":"4","name":"Nicki","ec2":"nicki"},{"id":"5","name":"Jedzenie","ec2":"jedzenie"},{"id":"6","name":"Powitania 

    // ==========================================
    // KONIEC SEKCJI DANYCH
    // ==========================================

    const URL_PREFIX = "https://i.iplsc.com/-/";
    const URL_SUFFIX = "-O0.gif";

    // Stan aplikacji
    let allGifs = [];
    let filteredGifs = [];
    let categories = {};
    let currentPage = 1;
    let pageSize = 100;

    window.onload = function() {
        if (!GIF_DATABASE) {
            const gallery = document.getElementById('gallery');
            gallery.innerHTML = `
                <div style="grid-column: 1/-1; text-align: center; padding: 50px;">
                    <h2>⚠️ Nie znaleziono danych</h2>
                    <p>Proszę edytować ten plik HTML.</p>
                    <p>Znajdź linię <code>const GIF_DATABASE = null;</code> i zastąp <code>null</code> zawartością Twojego pliku JSON.</p>
                </div>
            `;
            return;
        }
        parseDatabase(GIF_DATABASE);
    };

    function parseDatabase(json) {
        if (!json.data || !json.data.images_list || !json.data.categories_list) {
            alert("Błąd: Nieprawidłowa struktura pliku JSON.");
            return;
        }

        // Mapowanie Kategorii
        json.data.categories_list.forEach(cat => {
            categories[cat.id] = cat.name;
        });
        categories["default"] = "Pozostałe"; 

        // Przetwarzanie Obrazków
        allGifs = [];
        const imgList = json.data.images_list;

        for (let key in imgList) {
            // Identyfikacja kategorii
            let catId = "default";
            if (key.startsWith("cat")) {
                catId = key.replace("cat", "");
            }
            const catName = categories[catId] || "Bez kategorii";

            // Przetwarzanie elementów
            const items = imgList[key];
            if (Array.isArray(items)) {
                items.forEach(item => {
                    // format: ["u-code", "HASH"]
                    if (item.length >= 2) {
                        const code = item[0];
                        const hash = item[1];
                        allGifs.push({
                            code: `<${code}>`, // Surowy string do kopiowania
                            rawCode: code, 
                            url: URL_PREFIX + hash + URL_SUFFIX,
                            category: catName
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        populateCategoryDropdown();
        filterData();
    }

    function populateCategoryDropdown() {
        const select = document.getElementById('category-select');
        const uniqueCats = [...new Set(allGifs.map(g => g.category))].sort();
        
        uniqueCats.forEach(cat => {
            let opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = cat;
            opt.innerText = cat;
            select.appendChild(opt);
        });
    }

    function filterData() {
        const catSelect = document.getElementById('category-select').value;
        const searchTerm = document.getElementById('search-input').value.toLowerCase();

        filteredGifs = allGifs.filter(gif => {
            const matchesCat = (catSelect === 'all') || (gif.category === catSelect);
            const matchesSearch = gif.code.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm) || gif.rawCode.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);
            return matchesCat && matchesSearch;
        });

        currentPage = 1;
        renderGrid();
    }

    function handleSearch() { filterData(); }
    function changeCategory() { filterData(); }
    function changePageSize() {
        pageSize = parseInt(document.getElementById('page-size').value);
        currentPage = 1;
        renderGrid();
    }

    function renderGrid() {
        const gallery = document.getElementById('gallery');
        gallery.innerHTML = '';

        const totalItems = filteredGifs.length;
        const totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / pageSize);
        
        if (currentPage > totalPages) currentPage = totalPages || 1;

        const start = (currentPage - 1) * pageSize;
        const end = start + pageSize;
        const itemsToShow = filteredGifs.slice(start, end);

        itemsToShow.forEach(gif => {
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'gif-card';
            
            // Przekazujemy surowy kod do funkcji kopiowania
            card.onclick = () => copyToClipboard(gif.code);
            card.title = "Kliknij, aby skopiować kod";

            // WAŻNE: Zamiana znaków < i > na encje HTML, aby przeglądarka wyświetlała je jako tekst
            const displayCode = gif.code.replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");

            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="img-wrapper">
                    <img src="${gif.url}" loading="lazy" alt="${displayCode}">
                </div>
                <div class="code-badge">${displayCode}</div>
            `;
            gallery.appendChild(card);
        });

        updatePaginationControls(totalPages, totalItems);
    }

    function updatePaginationControls(totalPages, totalItems) {
        document.getElementById('page-info').innerText = `Strona ${currentPage} z ${totalPages} (${totalItems} GIFów)`;
        document.getElementById('btn-prev').disabled = (currentPage <= 1);
        document.getElementById('btn-next').disabled = (currentPage >= totalPages);
    }

    function nextPage() {
        currentPage++;
        renderGrid();
        document.getElementById('gallery-container').scrollTop = 0;
    }

    function prevPage() {
        currentPage--;
        renderGrid();
        document.getElementById('gallery-container').scrollTop = 0;
    }

    function copyToClipboard(text) {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
            showToast(`Skopiowano: ${text}`);
        });
    }

    function showToast(msg) {
        const toast = document.getElementById("toast");
        toast.innerText = msg;
        toast.className = "show";
        setTimeout(function(){ toast.className = toast.className.replace("show", ""); }, 3000);
    }
</script>

</body>
</html>
